This is a different resource, scoped to the parent resource, but it may have a different kind.\n    41→\t// For instance, /pods has the resource \"pods\" and the kind \"Pod\", while /pods/foo/status has the resource \"pods\", the sub resource \"status\", and the kind \"Pod\"\n    42→\t// (because status operates on pods). The binding resource for a pod though may be /pods/foo/binding, which has resource \"pods\", subresource \"binding\", and kind \"Binding\".\n    43→\tGetSubresource() string\n    44→\t// GetOperation is the operation being performed\n    45→\tGetOperation() Operation\n    46→\t// GetOperationOptions is the options for the operation being performed\n    47→\tGetOperationOptions() runtime.Object\n    48→\t// IsDryRun indicates that modifications will definitely not be persisted for this request. This is to prevent\n    49→\t// admission controllers with side effects and a method of reconciliation from being overwhelmed.\n    50→\t// However, a value of false for this does not mean that the modification will be persisted, because it\n    51→\t// could still be rejected by a subsequent validation step.\n    52→\tIsDryRun() bool\n    53→\t// GetObject is the object from the incoming request prior to default values being applied\n    54→\tGetObject() runtime.Object\n    55→\t// GetOldObject is the existing object. plugins in this flag does not matter.\")\n\tfs.StringVar(&a.ConfigFile, \"admission-control-config-file\", a.ConfigFile,\n\t\t\"File with admission control configuration.\")\n}\n\n// ApplyTo adds the admission chain to the server configuration.\n// In case admission plugin names were not provided by a cluster-admin they will be prepared from the recommended/default values.\n// In addition the method lazily initializes a generic plugin that is appended to the list of pluginInitializers\n// note this method uses:\n//\n//\tgenericconfig.Authorizer\nfunc (a *AdmissionOptions) ApplyTo(\n\tc *server.Config,\n\tinformers informers.SharedInformerFactory,\n\tkubeClient kubernetes.Interface,\n\tdynamicClient dynamic.Interface,\n\tfeatures featuregate.FeatureGate,\n\tpluginInitializers ...admission.PluginInitializer,\n) error {\n\tif a == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Admission depends on CoreAPI to set SharedInformerFactory and ClientConfig.\n\tif informers == nil depends on a Kubernetes core API client, it cannot be nil\")\n\t}\n\n\tpluginNames := a.enabledPluginNames()\n\n\tpluginsConfigProvider, err := admission.ReadAdmissionConfiguration(pluginNames, cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(kubeClient.Discovery())\n\tdiscoveryRESTMapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(discoveryClient)\n\tgenericInitializer := initializer.New(kubeClient, dynamicClient, informers, c.Authorization.Authorizer, features,\n\t\tc.DrainedNotify(), discoveryRESTMapper)\n\tinitializersChain := admission.PluginInitializers{genericInitializer}\n\tinitializersChain = append(initializersChain, pluginInitializers...)\n\n\tadmissionPostStartHook := func(hookContext server.PostStartHookContext) error {\n\t\tdiscoveryRESTMapper.Reset()\n\t\tgo utilwait.Until(discoveryRESTMapper.Reset, 30*time.Second, hookContext.Done())\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\terr = err)\n\t}\n\n\tadmissionChain, err := a.Plugins.NewFromPlugins(pluginNames, pluginsConfigProvider, initializersChain, a.Decorators)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tc.AdmissionControl = admissionmetrics.WithStepMetrics(admissionChain)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Validate verifies flags passed to AdmissionOptions.\nfunc (a *AdmissionOptions) Validate() []error {\n\tif a == nil disable-admission-plugins \"+\n\t\t\t\"overlapped\", enablePlugins.Intersection(disablePlugins).List()))\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify RecommendedPluginOrder.\n\trecommendPlugins := never run in.\n\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"plugins %v in RecommendedPluginOrder are not registered\",\n\t\t\trecommendPlugins.Difference(intersections).List()))\n\t}\n\tif RecommendedPluginOrder\",\n\t\t\tregisteredPlugins.Difference(intersections).List()))\n\t}\n\n\treturn errs\n}\n\n// enabledPluginNames makes use of RecommendedPluginOrder, DefaultOffPlugins,\n// EnablePlugins, DisablePlugins fields\n// to prepare a list of ordered plugin names that are enabled.\nfunc (a *AdmissionOptions) enabledPluginNames() []string {\n\tallOffPlugins := append(sets.List[string](a.DefaultOffPlugins), a.DisablePlugins...)\n\tdisabledPlugins := sets.NewString(allOffPlugins...)\n\tenabledPlugins := sets.NewString(a.EnablePlugins...)\n\tdisabledPlugins = disabledPlugins.Difference(enabledPlugins)\n\n\torderedPlugins := []string{}\n\tfor _, plugin := range a.RecommendedPluginOrder {\n\t\tif !disabledPlugins.Has(plugin) {\n\t\t\torderedPlugins = append(orderedPlugins, plugin)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn orderedPlugins\n}\n\n// Return names of plugins which are enabled by default\nfunc (a *AdmissionOptions) defaultEnabledPluginNames() []string {\n\tdefaultOnPluginNames := []string{}\n\tfor _, pluginName := range a.RecommendedPluginOrder {\n\t\tif !a.DefaultOffPlugins.Has(pluginName) {\n\t\t\tdefaultOnPluginNames = across multiple packages in kubernetes/kubernetes. Here's the comprehensive flow:\\n\\n## Core Admission Interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\nThe foundation is defined in **interfaces.go**, which declares three key interfaces:\\n- **Interface**: Base interface with Handles(operation) method\\n- **MutationInterface**: Extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admission\\n- **ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validating admission\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**chain.go** implements the core admission chain:\\n- **chainAdmissionHandler**: A []Interface that processes multiple admission handlers in sequence\\n- **Admit()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Validate()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support reinvocation:\\n- **newReinvocationHandler()**: Creates a wrapper that can reinvoke the admission chain if webhooks request re-invocation\\n- Checks reinvocation context after Admit() to determine if second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin factories\\n- **Register()**: Registers plugin factories by name\\n- **NewFromPlugins()**: Builds admission chain from plugin names, separates mutating/validating plugins, wraps with reinvocation handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including lifecycle, webhooks, and admission policies\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Ordering and Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing MutationInterface\\n- **Admit()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes mutating webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## Validating Admission Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages webhook configuration sources, HTTP client, namespace/object matchers\\n- Implements ValidateInitialization() to ensure proper setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go**:\\n- Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, sequence\\n- **Admit()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Validate()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. interfaces:\\n- **Interface**: Base interface with Handles(operation) method\\n- **MutationInterface**: Extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admission\\n- **ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validating admission\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**chain.go** implements the core admission chain:\\n- **chainAdmissionHandler**: A []Interface that processes multiple admission handlers in sequence\\n- **Admit()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Validate()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support reinvocation:\\n- **newReinvocationHandler()**: Creates a wrapper that can reinvoke the admission chain if webhooks request re-invocation\\n- Checks reinvocation context after Admit() to determine if second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin factories\\n- **Register()**: Registers plugin factories by name\\n- **NewFromPlugins()**: Builds admission chain from plugin names, separates mutating/validating plugins, wraps with reinvocation handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including lifecycle, webhooks, and admission policies\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Ordering and Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing MutationInterface\\n- **Admit()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes mutating webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API request arrives:\\n1. Here's the comprehensive flow:\\n\\n## Core Admission Interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\nThe foundation is defined in **interfaces.go**, which declares three key interfaces:\\n- **Interface**: Base interface with Handles(operation) method\\n- **MutationInterface**: Extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admission\\n- **ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validating admission\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**chain.go** implements the core admission chain:\\n- **chainAdmissionHandler**: A []Interface that processes multiple admission handlers in sequence\\n- **Admit()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Validate()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support reinvocation:\\n- **newReinvocationHandler()**: Creates a wrapper that can reinvoke the admission chain if webhooks request re-invocation\\n- Checks reinvocation context after Admit() to determine if second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin factories\\n- **Register()**: Registers plugin factories by name\\n- **NewFromPlugins()**: Builds admission chain from plugin names, separates mutating/validating plugins, wraps with reinvocation handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including lifecycle, webhooks, and admission policies\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go** implements:\\n- **WithStepMetrics()**: Decorator that wraps the admission chain to record admission metrics\\n- Used to track admission latency, rejections, and errors per plugin\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Ordering and Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing MutationInterface\\n- **Admit()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes mutating webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## Validating Admission Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages webhook configuration sources, HTTP client, namespace/object matchers\\n- Implements ValidateInitialization() to ensure proper setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go**:\\n- Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook]\\n\\n## Kube-apiserver Specific Implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**:\\n- Wraps generic AdmissionOptions with kube-apiserver specific configuration\\n- Delegates to generic ApplyTo() implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go**:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (21 in-tree plugins)\\n- **AllOrderedPlugins**: Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed, may re-run mutations\\n5. API server calls AdmissionControl.Validate() on the reinvocation handler\\n6. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. Handlers are ordered by plugin registration, with mutations always before validations\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":72,"oldLines":5,"newStart":72,"newLines":5,"lines":["     {\"repo\": \"kubernetes/kubernetes\", \"path\": \"staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/dispatcher.go\", \"symbol\": \"Dispatch\"},","     {\"repo\": \"kubernetes/kubernetes\", \"path\": \"staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go\", \"symbol\": \"ApplyTo\"}","   ],","-  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission controller pipeline is implemented across multiple packages in kubernetes/kubernetes. packages in kubernetes/kubernetes. Here's the comprehensive flow:\\n\\n## Core Admission Interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\nThe foundation is defined in **interfaces.go**, which declares three key interfaces:\\n- **Interface**: Base interface with Handles(operation) method\\n- **MutationInterface**: Extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admission\\n- **ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validating admission\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**chain.go** implements the core admission chain:\\n- **chainAdmissionHandler**: A []Interface that processes multiple admission handlers in sequence\\n- **Admit()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Validate()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support reinvocation:\\n- **newReinvocationHandler()**: Creates a wrapper that can reinvoke the admission chain if webhooks request re-invocation\\n- Checks reinvocation context after Admit() to determine if second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin factories\\n- **Register()**: Registers plugin factories by name\\n- **NewFromPlugins()**: Builds admission chain from plugin names, separates mutating/validating plugins, wraps with reinvocation handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including lifecycle, webhooks, and admission policies\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go** implements:\\n- **WithStepMetrics()**: Decorator that wraps the admission chain to record admission metrics\\n- Used to track admission latency, rejections, and errors per plugin\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Ordering and Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing MutationInterface\\n- **Admit()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes mutating webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## Validating Admission Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Admission Policies (CEL-based Rules)\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing MutationInterface\\n- **Admit()** method that delegates to policy dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionPolicy plugin\\n- Evaluates CEL rules to apply mutations using JSONPatch\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **Dispatcher** implementation that evaluates mutating policies\\n- Compiles CEL rules and applies patches to requests\\n- Supports policy composition and ordering\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to policy dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers ValidatingAdmissionPolicy plugin\\n- Evaluates CEL rules to validate requests\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **Dispatcher** implementation that evaluates validating policies\\n- Compiles CEL rules and returns validation errors\\n- Supports policy composition and ordering\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages webhook configuration sources, HTTP client, namespace/object matchers\\n- Implements ValidateInitialization() to ensure proper setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go**:\\n- Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup and Integration\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/config.go**:\\n- **Config** struct has AdmissionControl field (admission.Interface)\\n- AdmissionControl is stored in REST handler context\\n- Used to process all requests through the admission pipeline\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), wraps with metrics decorator, applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook]\"\\n\\n## Kube-apiserver Specific Implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**:\\n- Wraps generic AdmissionOptions with kube-apiserver specific configuration\\n- Delegates to generic ApplyTo() implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go**:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (21 in-tree plugins)\\n- **AllOrderedPlugins**: Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed, may re-run mutations\\n5. API server calls AdmissionControl.Validate() on the reinvocation handler\\n6. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), wraps with metrics decorator, applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: Implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**:\\n- Wraps generic AdmissionOptions with kube-apiserver specific configuration\\n- Delegates to generic ApplyTo() implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go**:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (21 in-tree plugins)\\n- **AllOrderedPlugins**: Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and Records admission latency, rejections, and errors per plugin\\n- Decorators are applied in inside-out order during ApplyTo()\\n- Metrics decorator wraps individual handlers to instrument admission pipeline\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives at the API server:\\n1. REST handler calls AdmissionControl.Admit() (wrapped by metrics decorator and reinvocation handler)\\n2. Metrics decorator records start time for this step\\n3. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n4. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - NamespaceLifecycle (namespace existence checks)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based mutation rules)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that mutate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n5. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed:\\n   - If any mutating handler set ShouldReinvoke flag, re-run mutations\\n   - Allows webhooks to react to mutations from other webhooks\\n6. REST handler calls AdmissionControl.Validate()\\n7. Metrics decorator records start time for validation step\\n8. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n9. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based validation rules)\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that validate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n10. Metrics decorator records latency and reports success/failure\\n11. Returns to REST handler with admission decision\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Chain of Responsibility**: Multiple handlers form a chain, each can process or reject requests\\n- **Separation of Concerns**: Mutating handlers always run before validating handlers\\n- **Decorator Pattern**: Metrics, decorators wrap handlers to add cross-cutting concerns\\n- **Factory Pattern**: Plugins.Register() and NewFromPlugins() create chains from named plugins\\n- **Reinvocation Policy**: Webhooks can request re-invocation to react to mutations\\n- **Configuration Driven**: Plugins loaded via configuration, not hard-coded\\n\""," }"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

context\\n- Used to process all requests through the admission pipeline\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, Records admission latency, rejections, and errors per plugin\\n- Decorators are applied in inside-out order during ApplyTo()\\n- Metrics decorator wraps individual handlers to instrument admission pipeline\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives at the API server:\\n1. REST handler calls AdmissionControl.Admit() (wrapped by metrics decorator and reinvocation handler)\\n2. Metrics decorator records start time for this step\\n3. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n4. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - NamespaceLifecycle (namespace existence checks)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based mutation rules)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that mutate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n5. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed:\\n   - If any mutating handler set ShouldReinvoke flag, re-run mutations\\n   - Allows webhooks to react to mutations from other webhooks\\n6. REST handler calls AdmissionControl.Validate()\\n7. Metrics decorator records start time for validation step\\n8. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n9. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based validation rules)\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that validate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n10. Metrics decorator records latency and reports success/failure\\n11. Returns to REST handler with admission decision\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Chain of Responsibility**: Multiple handlers form a chain, each can process or reject requests\\n- **Separation of Concerns**: Mutating handlers always run before validating handlers\\n- **Decorator Pattern**: Metrics, decorators wrap handlers to add cross-cutting concerns\\n- **Factory Pattern**: Plugins.Register() and NewFromPlugins() create chains from named plugins\\n- **Reinvocation Policy**: Webhooks can request re-invocation to react to mutations\\n- **Configuration Driven**: Plugins loaded via configuration, not hard-coded\\n\"\n}\n","numLines":77,"startLine":1,"totalLines":77}}}
